<heading>

26.  CMMIRK-M34,114.3123

DOMINICA IN RAMIS PALMARUM SERMO BREUIS.  CMMIRK-M34,114.3124

<$$heading>

Cristen men and woymen, as +ge knowy+te well, +tys day is called
Palme-Sonday.  CMMIRK-M34,114.3126

But for bycause +tat +te seruyce of +tys day is so long, I woll schortly
tell you whi +tys day is called soo.  CMMIRK-M34,114.3127

Thys day, as Seynt Ion telly+te, our Lord Ihesu Crist was in Bethany wher
he reisyd a mon from de+te to lyue +tat had layne four dayes stynkyng
yn +te tombe, +tat was called La+garus, and was bro+tyr to Mary Mawdelen
and Martha, hyr sustyr.  CMMIRK-M34,114.3128

Then wist Ihesu Crist hys passion was negh, CMMIRK-M34,114.3129

and toke La+gar wyth hym, CMMIRK-M34,114.3130

and so rydyng on an asse +gode to Ierusalem.  CMMIRK-M34,114.3131

And when +te pepull herdyn +tat, all +goden a+geynes hym, bo+te for
<P_115> wondyr of +te mon +tat was raysud from de+te to lyue, and also
forto do Crist worschip.  Wherfor mony strawed flowres in hys way,
and mony broken branches of olyue and of palme and keston in +te way,
and spradden clo+tys in +te way, makyng melody and syngyng +tus:'
Blessid be +tou +tat comys in +te name of our Lord, Kyng of Israel!
'Wherfor holy chyrch, +tys day, make+te a solemp procescyon in mynd
of +tat procescyon +tat Crist made +tis day, and also for mony of you
ben raysed from de+te to lyue +tat han leyn four dayes dede, +tat ben
synfull +toghtys, synfull speches, synfull werkes, and synfull customs.
CMMIRK-M34,115.3132

But now I hope +tat +ge ben reysed from de+te of euel lyuyng to +te
lyfe of grace, and +tat angeles yn Heuen maken as moche melody yn Heuen
for your arysyng as +te pepull dyd for wondyr of rysyng of +te La+gare.
CMMIRK-M34,115.3133

But for bycause we haue no olyf +tat beren grene leues, we taken ive
instede of that and palmes CMMIRK-M34,115.3134

and beren about on procession; CMMIRK-M34,115.3135

and so +tys day we callne Palme-Sonday.  CMMIRK-M34,115.3136

And as +tay songen and duden worschip to Crist in hor procescyon, ry+gt
soo we worschip +tis day +te cros yn our procescyon, +trys knelyng to +te
cros yn worschip and in mynd of hym +tat was for vs don on +te crosse,
and welcomyng hym wyth songe into +te chirch, as +tay welcomet hym
syngyng into +te cyte of Ierusalem.  CMMIRK-M34,115.3137

+Ten asky+te Ion Belet a qwestion:'Sy+ten +tat Crist had +te grattest
worschyp ridyng on an asse +tat euer he had in +tys world, and aftyr of
+te same pepull was don on +te cros in +te grattest vyleny +tat euer
he had {TEXT:ha} yn +tys world, whi we worschip +te cros, and not +te
asse? 'CMMIRK-M34,115.3138

To +tys qwestion he vnswares hymselfe CMMIRK-M34,115.3139

and say+te +tat all +te worschip of +tys world turny+te all to vanyte
and to no+gt, and maky+te a man bo+te to for+geton hys God and hymselfe,
$+ter $as {TEXT:+teras} myschef and woo maky+te a man to thynke on hys
God and to know hymselfe.  CMMIRK-M34,115.3140

Herefor, cristen men, putty+te away vanyte +tat bryngy+te a man to
euerlastyng payne, CMMIRK-M34,115.3141

and worschipy+te +te cros +tat was cause of our saluacyon and +te ioy
+tat we all hopyn forto come to.  CMMIRK-M34,115.3142

Then, when Crist was comen into +te cyte, anon he +gode into +te tempull,
CMMIRK-M34,115.3143

and drof out all byers and sellers +tat he fonde <P_116> +teryn
CMMIRK-M34,116.3144

and sayde to hom:'My fadyrs house ys a hous of prayers and of oresons ,
and +ge han made hyt a den of +teues'; +geuyng ych cristyn man hegh
ensampull forto leue chaffaryng on Sonday, and namly in chirch.
CMMIRK-M34,116.3145

Ano+tyr skyll ys whi +tys day is called Palme-Sonday, for bycause palme
bytokeny+te victory.  Wherfor ych cristyn man and woman schall +tys day
bere palmes yn processyon, schewyng +tat he ha+te foghten wyth +te fend,
and ha+te +te vyctory of hym by clene schryft of mow+te and repentans
of hert, and mekely don his penance, and in +tis wyse ouercome his enmy.
CMMIRK-M34,116.3146

<heading>

Narracio.  CMMIRK-M34,116.3148

<$$heading>

Hit was +te maner, summe tyme, as we redyn in +te Gestys of +te Romayns,
+tat when any lond of the world ros a+geyne +te Emperour of Rome, anon +te
Emperour wold send a wor+ty knyght wyth pepull ynogh to +tat lond, forto
set hyt downe and make hit soget to +te Emperour.  CMMIRK-M34,116.3150

And when +te kny+gt had so don, +ten schuld he be set in a chayre, as
ryaly as he my+gt, wyth clo+tys of gold drawyn ouer hym and a palme in
hys hond, schewyng +tat he had +te victory, CMMIRK-M34,116.3151

and so wyth gret worschip schuld be lad a+geyne to Rome.
CMMIRK-M34,116.3152

But when he come +trogh any cyte, +ter schuld a man stond by hym in
+te char, and bete hym in +te mowth wyth a branche of olyf, sayng +tus:
'Anothe selitos'; +tat is to say:'Know thyselfe. 'As +togh he sayde to
hym +tus: +tagh +tou haue +te victory now, hit may happen +tat +tou schalt
ano+tyr tyme have +te wors, and so turne +te in as moch vyleny as now +tis
do+te to worschip; wherfor be not prowde of +tyselfe.  CMMIRK-M34,116.3153

Thus, good men and woymen, +ge schull bete yourselfe in +te mow+te of
your soule wythyn-forth wyth +te branch of olyfe, +tat ys, wyth +te
uertu of mekenes.  CMMIRK-M34,116.3154

And soo hold mekenes in hert, beyng allway adred, lest +ge fall a+geyne to
your synne, and soo lese +te worschyp +tat +ge haue now ywonon, wittyng
well +tat mekenes ys +te vertu +tat most ouercomen your enmy, and most
growndy+t a man in doyng good werk and vertu.  Wherfor +ge schull all now
pray to God +tat he woll of his hygh grace +geue you myght and streng+te
in tyme comyng soo to ouercome your enmy, +tat +ge may haue +te victory
of hym, and haue +te blys +tat euer schall last.  CMMIRK-M34,116.3155

Amen.  CMMIRK-M34,116.3156

<heading>

27.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3159

SERMO ISTE DEBET DICI AD TENEBRAS.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3160

<$$heading>

Good men and woymen, as +ge se holy chyrch vsy+te +tes +tre dayes,
forto say seruyce in +te euentyde in derkenes.  Wherfor hyt ys called
wyth you teneblus; CMMIRK-M34,117.3162

but holy chyrch cally+te hit tenebras, +tat is to say, derkenes.
CMMIRK-M34,117.3163

Then why +tys seruyce is don in derkenes, holy fadyrs wryty+te to vs
+tre skylles.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3164

On skyll ys, for bycause +tat Crist +tys nyght, before +tat he was taken,
he +gode +tries ynto +te hull of Olyuete, CMMIRK-M34,117.3165

and prayde his fadyr to put away +te hard payne +tat hym was toward,
yf hit wer his wyll and elles not; CMMIRK-M34,117.3166

and soo, for drede of +te passion +tat he feld in his spyryte comyng,
he swat blod and watyr.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3167

Ano+tyr skyll ys, for anon, aftyr mydny+gt, Iudas gedyrd knyghtys,
strong and bold, wyth o+tyr gret company of mysdoers, and comen forto

But for hyt was derke nyght, and +tay cow+te not well know Crist by Saynt

lest +tay hadden taken Iames ynsted of Crist, Iudas bade hom take hym
+tat he kyssud.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3169

And soo wyth a kysse betrayde hys maystyr.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3170

And so token Crist all in darkenes, CMMIRK-M34,117.3171

and dydden hym all +te despyte and vylany yn bobbyng and spyttyng yn
hys louely face.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3172

Tho +tryd skyll ys, for when Crist was naylet fote and hond, hongyng on
+te cros, +tre oures of +te day from vndure to none, +te sonne wythdro+g
hyr ly+gt CMMIRK-M34,117.3173

and was darke +trogh +te world, schewyng +tat +te maker of ly+gt payned
+tat tyme to de+te.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3174

For +tes +tre skylles +te seruyce of +tes +tre nyghtys is don yn darkenes.
+Te whech seruyce maky+te mynd how Iudas be-trayde Crist, and how +tes
Iewes comen wyth fors and armes as priuely as +tay cow+t, for drede of
+te pepull.  Wherfor to +tys seruyce ys no bell rongyn, but a sowne made
of tre wherby ych cristen man and woman is enformed, forto com to +tys
seruyce wythout noyse makyng.  CMMIRK-M34,117.3175

And all +tat +tay spekyn, goyng and comyng, schall sowne of +te tre
+tat Crist was don on, and of +te <P_118> wordes +te whech Crist spake

how he betoke his soule ynto his fadyr hond, and so +gelde vp +te gost.
CMMIRK-M34,118.3176

+Tus, goyng and comyng to +tys seruyce, ych cristen man and woman
schall leue talkyng of all vanyte, and only talke of +te cros.
CMMIRK-M34,118.3177

Ano+tyr skyll is, when +tat Iudas had trayde Crist, and sy+g +tat
by his traytery he schuld be ded, anon he fell ynto dyspayre, and
+gode and hongyd hymself on a tre, so +tat he wra+tut Crist more for
hongyng hymselfe yn dyspayre, +ten dyd +te traytery +tat he dyd befor.
CMMIRK-M34,118.3178

For Crist is so mercyabull in hymself, +tat he wold haue +gyuen hym mercy
, and he wold haue askyd hyt wyth contryte hert.  CMMIRK-M34,118.3179

Also at +tys seruyce is set a hers wyth candull brennyng, aftyr as +te vse
ys som plase moo, summe las.  +Te whech ben qwenched ych on aftyr o+tyr,
yn schewyng how Cristis dyscypull stelen from hym, when he was taken,
yche on aftyr o+tyr.  CMMIRK-M34,118.3180

But when all ben quenchyd, +get on leue+te lyght.  +Te whech ys borne away

CMMIRK-M34,118.3181

Then, aftyr +tys, +te candyll ys broght a+geyne, and all o+tyr at hit

of lyfe to all hom +tat werne qwenchit by dyspayre.  CMMIRK-M34,118.3182

+Te strokes +tat +te prest +geuy+t on +te boke bytokeny+te +te clappys
of +tondyr +tat Crist brake hell-+gatys wyth, when he com +tedyr and
spylud hom.  CMMIRK-M34,118.3183

Now, good men, +ge haue herde what +tys seruyce betokeny+te.  Wherfor
holdu+te hit in your hert, and be +ge not vnkynd to your God, +tat +tus
suffryd for you; CMMIRK-M34,118.3184

for vnkyndnes ys a synne +tat he haty+t he+gly.  Wherfor Seynt Ambros
say+te +tat +ter may no man fynde a payne, forto poynych dewly +te vyce

<P_119>

<heading>

Narracio.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3188

<$$heading>

An ensampull of +tys I fynd, as Alisandyr Nekkam telle+te,
CMMIRK-M34,119.3190

and is +tys.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3191

+Ter was summe tyme a kny+gt +tat went out of his contrey into ferre
contray, forto sech aventurs.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3192

And so hyt fell +tat he come into a gret forest and herd a gret noyse
of a best +tat was, as hym +to+gt, in gret dystres.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3193

Then, for he wold se what hit was, he +gode nygh CMMIRK-M34,119.3194

and sech how an horrybull neddyr of gretnes and of leng+te had
vmbeclyppyd a lyon, and soo bond hym to a tre as he lened hym to slepe.
CMMIRK-M34,119.3195

hymselfe, he made an hygys noyse; CMMIRK-M34,119.3196

and when he saw +tys knyght, +ten made he grettyr noyse, wilnyng helpe
of hym.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3197

Then had +tys kny+gt compassyon of +tys lyon, CMMIRK-M34,119.3198

CMMIRK-M34,119.3203

and lay at his bedys fete ych ny+gt, CMMIRK-M34,119.3204

and in ich turment and batayle he helpe hys maystyr; soo +tat all men
speken of +tys knyght and of +tys lyon.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3205

+Get, by counsell of summe men, he had +tys lyon yn suspescyon.  Wherfor
when he +gode a+geyne hom to hys one contre, priuelych, wyll +te lyon
slepte, he +gode into a schyp, and soo saylet forth.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3206

But when +te lyon woke and myst hys maystyr, anon he +gaf a gret rore,
CMMIRK-M34,119.3207

and +gode aftyr hym to +te see; CMMIRK-M34,119.3208

CMMIRK-M34,119.3209

and when his my+gt fayled hym, +ten was he drowned.  CMMIRK-M34,119.3210

By +tys kny+gt we may vndyrstond Crist, Godys sonne of Heuen, +tat

CMMIRK-M34,120.3211

<heading>

28.  CMMIRK-M34,120.3215

SERMO DICENDUS AD PAROCHIANOS IN PARASCEUE DOMINI HOC MODO.
CMMIRK-M34,120.3216

<$$heading>

Cristen men and women, +ge schull vndyrstond +tat Crist +tys day sched
hys hert-blod for vs.  CMMIRK-M34,120.3218

As +ge all knowen wele, +tys day is called Good Fryday;
CMMIRK-M34,120.3219

for all +tyng turned +te pepull to good +tat Crist +tys day suffryd for
hom vndyr Pounce Pylat.  CMMIRK-M34,120.3220

Then, for hyt ys oft sene, all euell bygynnyng ha+te a foule

CMMIRK-M34,120.3221

and for he began cursetly, he endyd wrecchedly.  CMMIRK-M34,120.3222

+Ten aftyr +tat he was +tre +ger old, +te modyr bro+gt hym to +te kyngys
court to his fadyr.  CMMIRK-M34,120.3228

CMMIRK-M34,120.3229

But for +tys chyld was yn all doyng more gentyll and more monfall,

and on a day wayted his tyme, CMMIRK-M34,120.3237

CMMIRK-M34,121.3239

and soo gate his nome CMMIRK-M34,121.3241

and was called Pylat of Ponse.  CMMIRK-M34,121.3242

and made hym lefetenant vndyr hym of all his lond of Iury.
CMMIRK-M34,121.3244

Then, for Pylat lyked well +tat offyce, priuely he send to +te Emperour
CMMIRK-M34,121.3245

and had his office confermyd of hym, vnwyttyng of Herod +te kyng.
Wherfor Herode and he wern enmys tyll +te tyme +tat Crist was taken;
CMMIRK-M34,121.3246

and soo in +te assent of Cristys de+te +tay becom frendys.
CMMIRK-M34,121.3247

CMMIRK-M34,121.3249

+Ten was Pylat adred CMMIRK-M34,121.3250

29.  CMMIRK-M34,124.3331

SERMO ISTE SEQUENS NON DICENDUS EST AD PARASCEUES, SED QUAEDAM FORMACIO
NECESSARIA CAPELLANIS.  HOC MODO.  CMMIRK-M34,124.3332

<$$heading>

For hyt ys $oft ysene +tat lewde men +te wheche bu+te of mony wordys
and proude in hor wit, woll aske prestes dyuerse questyons of +tynges
+tat towchen to seruyce of holy chyrche, and namly of +tys tyme, and
gladly suche prestys as con not make a gray+te vnswar so, forto put hom
to aschame, wherfor I haue tytuld here dyuerse poyntys whech +tat byn
nedfull to yche prest to know.  CMMIRK-M34,124.3334

So he +tat woll loke and hold hit yn hys hert, <P_125> he may make
an vnswar, soo +tat he schall do hymselfe worschyp and o+tyr profyt.
CMMIRK-M34,125.3335

Furst, yf a man aske why Schere +Tursday ys called soo, say +tat in holy
chyrch hit is called our Lordys supperday.  CMMIRK-M34,125.3336

For $+tylke day he sowped wyth hys dyscypuls openly; CMMIRK-M34,125.3337

drynke; CMMIRK-M34,125.3338

in hym and +te gret loue +tat he had to hom.  CMMIRK-M34,125.3339

and dodde hor heddys, CMMIRK-M34,125.3342

+Ten, from +te font, men gon to +te qwere syngyng +te letany, prayng
all +te sayntys of Heuen forto pray to God, +geue hom +tat ben folowed
grace forto kepe +te he+g couenant +tat +tay haue made in hor folowyng.
CMMIRK-M34,128.3417

Then men gon to masse +tat is bygonnen wythout office, +tat is called
+te hed of +te masse; CMMIRK-M34,128.3418

for Crist, +tat is hed of all holy chyrch, ys not +get risen from de+t
to lyue.  CMMIRK-M34,128.3419

Kyrieleyson is sayd; CMMIRK-M34,128.3420

for in iche office of holy chyrch, and namly yn +te masse, hit ys
gret nede forto aske helpe and socour of God, forto defende vs out of
temptacyon +tat assayly+t vs namly in Godys seruyce.  CMMIRK-M34,128.3421

<P_129>

'Gloria in excelsis'ys sayde; CMMIRK-M34,129.3423

for +te Fadyr of Heuen is gretly ioyet forto behold +te pepull +tat his
sonne ha+te bo+gt wyth hys passyon, +tat lyuen in charyte and in pes,
ych on wyth o+tyr.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3424

Grayle is non sayde; CMMIRK-M34,129.3425

for +tylke +tat ben folowed, be not +get parfyte to walke yn +te greus
of vertu.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3426

Alleluia ys songen; CMMIRK-M34,129.3427

for hyt ys gret ioy to angeles to sen +te ruyne of angeles be restowred
by +tylke +tat ben folowed.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3428

Aftyr Alleluia +te tracte ys songen; CMMIRK-M34,129.3429

for +tagh +tay ben, in hor folo+gt, waschan of all synnys, +get +tay
most travayle bysyly, forto kepe hom out of combrans of +te fend, +tat
he fall not into dedly synne a+geyne.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3430

Offertory is non sayde; CMMIRK-M34,129.3431

for +te wymmen +tat comen, forto offyr to Cristys body oynmentes, +tay
fond hym not in his tombe.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3432

'Agnus Dei'ys sayde, CMMIRK-M34,129.3433

but no pax ys borne; CMMIRK-M34,129.3434

for Crist +tat is hed of pes, was not +get rysen.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3435

Postcomyn is non sayde; CMMIRK-M34,129.3436

for +tay +tat ben folowed schul not be howsyld +tys day, but on +te
morow; CMMIRK-M34,129.3437

for in +te begynnyng of holy chirch +ter comen moo to folow of gret age
+ten of chyldren.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3438

A schort euensong ys don, lest +tay +tat ben folowet for cold o+tyr
sekenes wer anyet of long seruyce.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3439

+Ten is all +tys seruyce endyd vndyr on colet for all +te sacra-ment of
holy chirch, CMMIRK-M34,129.3440

and of folo+gt is endyd in +te passion of Crist.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3441

<heading>

30.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3443

DE FESTO PASCHE.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3444

<$$heading>

Cristes pepull, bo+te men and woymen, as +ge all knowen wele, +tys day
is called in sum place Astyr-day, and in sum plase Pase-day, and in sum
plas Godis Sonday.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3446

Hyt is called Astyr-day, as Candylmas-day of candyls, and Palme-Sonday
of palmes.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3447

For wel nygh in ych plase, hyt ys +te maner +tys day forto do fyre out
of +te hall at +te astyr, +tat ha+te all +te wyntyr brent wyth fyre and
blakyd wyth smoke.  CMMIRK-M34,129.3448

Hit schall +tys day ben arayde wyth grene rusches, and swete flowres
strawed all aboute, schewyng an hegh ensampull to all men and woymen +tat
, ryght as +tay maken clene +te howse all wythyn, beryng out +te fure and
strawyng flowres, ry+gt soo +ge schull clanse +te howse of your soule,
<P_130> doyng away +te fyre of lechery and of dedly wra+t and of envy,
and straw +ter swete erbes and flowres; CMMIRK-M34,130.3449

and +tat ben vertues of goodnes and of mekenes, of kyndnes, of loue and
charite, of pes and of rest: CMMIRK-M34,130.3450

and soo make +te howse of your soule abull to receyue your God.
CMMIRK-M34,130.3451

For ry+gt as +ge wyll not suffyr no +tyng in your howse +tat stynky+te or
saueryth euell, wherby +tat +ge may be dosesyd; ryght soo Crist, when he
comy+t into +te hows of your soule, and fyndeth +ter any stynkyng +tyng
of wra+t or of envy or any o+tyr dedly synne, he woll not abyde +ter:
CMMIRK-M34,130.3452

but anon he go+te out, CMMIRK-M34,130.3453

and +te fende comy+te yn CMMIRK-M34,130.3454

and abydy+te +ter.  CMMIRK-M34,130.3455

Then may +tat soule be full sory +tat scho ys forsaken of God and betaken
to +te fende.  CMMIRK-M34,130.3456

+Tus don +tay +tat holden dedly wra+te and dedly envy in hor hertys,
and woll not for+geue +tylk +tat haue trespast to hom, for no prayer.
Wherfor take hit wyth certeyne: CMMIRK-M34,130.3457

+togh +ge mow wyth glosyng wordys desayve me, and say +ge ben yn full
charyte as +ge owen forto be, +togh +ge be not soo, you gayne+t not
forto begyle God, +tat se+te ych cornell of your hertys.  Wherfor, for
Godys loue, dessayue +ge not yourselfe, but bu+te all besy forto kepe
your soules clene wythyn to Godis sy+gt, as +ge ben {busy} to make your
house clene to mannys sy+gt.  CMMIRK-M34,130.3458

And ryght as +ge clo+tu+t your astyr wyth fresche flowres and swete,
ry+gt so clo+te your astyr of your soule, +tat is, your hert, in fayr
clo+te of charyte, and of loue, and of pes, and of rest wyth all Godys
pepull, +tat +ge mow abull be forto receyve +te best frende +tat +ge
haue , +tat is Crist, Godis sonne of Heuen, +tat +tys tyme suffred de+te,
forto bryng you to +te lyfe +tat euer schall last.  CMMIRK-M34,130.3459

This day is also callyd Pase-day, +tat is in Englysch, +te passyng day.
CMMIRK-M34,130.3460

And soo hyt is for two skylles: CMMIRK-M34,130.3461

on for +tys day ych cristen man, in reuerence of God, schuld for+geue
+tat haue gylt to hom, and ben in full loue and charyte to Godis pepull
passyng all o+ter dayes of +te +gere; CMMIRK-M34,130.3462

for all +tat is mysdon all +te +gere befor, schall be helyd +tys day
wyth +te salue of charyte.  CMMIRK-M34,130.3463

Hit ys alsoo a passyng day: for ych Godys chyld schall passe out of
euell levyng into good lyuyng, out of vyces ynto vertuys, out of pride
into mekenes, out of couetyse into largenes, out of slo+t into holy
bysynes, out of envy into loue and charite, out of wra+te into mercy,
out of gloteny into abstynens, out of lechery into charyte, out of +te
fendys clochus ynto Godis barm; and soo of Godys <P_131> enmy make hym
hys frende and derlyng.  CMMIRK-M34,131.3464

Whoso passy+te +tus, he ys wor+ty forto come to +tat gret fest +tat God
maky+te +tys day to all +tat +tys passage makut.  CMMIRK-M34,131.3465

This day ys called Godis Sonday; for Crist, Godis sonne of Heuen,
+tys day roos from de+t to lyue, and soo glady+t all hys seruantes and
frendys wyth his vprist.  Wherfor all holy chrych maky+te myr+t +tys day
and syngyth +tus:'This ys +te day +tat our lord made; CMMIRK-M34,131.3466

be we glad and ioyfull in hure! 'CMMIRK-M34,131.3467

+Te Fadyr of Heuen makyth wyth all hys angelys soo gret melody for
+te vpryst of hys sonne, +tat he maky+te +tys day a gret passyng fest,
and byddy+te all hys pepull +terto, als wele hom +tat ben in Heuen as
+tylke +tat ben in er+te.  CMMIRK-M34,131.3468

+Ten as wele as hym schall be +tat comy+te to +tys fest wele arayde
in Godys lyuere, clo+tyd in loue and scharyte, als euell schall hym
be +tat comy+te yn fendys lyuere, clo+tyd in envy and dedly wra+te;
CMMIRK-M34,131.3469

for +tes, as +te gospell telly+te, schall be taken and cast into +te
prison of hell.  Soo that while o+tyr lagh and make mery, +tes o+tyr
wepe and be sory; CMMIRK-M34,131.3470

and whyll +tat o+tyr eten and drynken at Godis bord, +tay schall sytte
grennyng wyth hor te+te for paynyng of hell-wormys +tat gnawen hom.
CMMIRK-M34,131.3471

For as +tey eten o+tyr wyth bakbytyng here in er+te, +tey schull ete
hym backe and body wythout end in payne of hell.  Wherfor, good men
and woymen, I charch you heyly in Godys byhalue +tat non of you to-day
com to Godys bord, but he be in full charyte to all Godis pepull; and
also +tat +ge be clene schryuen and yn full wyll to leue your synne.
CMMIRK-M34,131.3472

For yf I wyst whech of you wer out of charyte and vnschryuen, I most,
be techyng of holy men, wyth a foule mou+te say +tus to hym, in audyens
of all men:'I +geue +te here not +ty howsyll, but +ty dampnacyon into
euerlastyng payne, tyll +tou com to amendement. 'Wherfor, for Cristis
loue, yche man sech well his conciens and clanse hyt, +tat he may abull
receyue hys sauyour.  CMMIRK-M34,131.3473

And +get, forto styr you more in concyens, y tell you +tys ensampull.
CMMIRK-M34,131.3474

<heading>

Narracio.  CMMIRK-M34,131.3476

<$$heading>

I rede of a holy byschop +tat prayd God bysily to +geue hym grace to
wytte whech wer wor+ty to receyue +te sacrament and whech onworthy.
CMMIRK-M34,131.3478

Then, when +te pepull com to Godys bord, he <P_132> sagh som com wyth
hor face red as blod, and blod droppyng out of hor mow+tys, som hor face
as blacke as any pyche, summe as whyte as snow, and summe fayre and rody
and lusty forto behold.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3479

Then, among o+tyr, he sagh two comyn wymen comyng and hor facys schonyng
as bryght as +te sonne.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3480

+Ten had he moch wondyr of +tys syght, CMMIRK-M34,132.3481

and prayde to God to +geue hym reuelacyon and knowyng what all +tys
bytokenyd.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3482

Then come +ter an angyll to hym CMMIRK-M34,132.3483

and sayd:'+Tes +tat han blody facys and blod droppe out of hor
mow+tes, +to ben envyous men and woymen, and full of dedly wra+te,
CMMIRK-M34,132.3484

and woll not amend hom, CMMIRK-M34,132.3485

and gnawen hom byhynd, CMMIRK-M34,132.3486

and be vsed to swere horrybull o+tys by Godys sydys and his blod,
and vmbrayden God of his passyon, and don hym no reuerence: wherfor
hor mow+tys schull droppe of blod, tyll +tay com to amendement.
CMMIRK-M34,132.3487

+Tay +tat haue blak facys, ben lecherys men and woymen +tat wyll not
leue hor synne, ne hor lyst, ne schryue hom +terof.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3488

+Tay +tat haue whit facys as snow, ben +tay +tat haue don gret synnys ,
and ben schryuen +terof, and wyth +te wepyng of hor een han wasshen hor
soules so whyt and clene.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3489

+Tylke +tat ben fayre and rody, ben good comyn lyuers +tat lyuen truly
by hor mayn swynke, CMMIRK-M34,132.3490

and so kepy+te hom out of dedly synne.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3491

And +tes two woymen +tat schynen passyng all o+tyr, wer two comyn woymen
and of euell lyuyng; CMMIRK-M34,132.3492

but when +tay come into +te chyrch, +tay toke suche repentans in hor
hertys, +tat +tay maden a vow to God +tat +tay wold do neuermore amys
wyth +te helpe of his grace.  Wherfor God of hys mercy ha+t for+geuen
hom hor synne, and so clene wasschen hor sowles, +tat +tay schyne +tus
passyng all o+ter. 'CMMIRK-M34,132.3493

Then +tys angyll went his way, CMMIRK-M34,132.3494

and +tys byschop +tonkyd God of hys hegh grace +tat he schewed hym
reuelacyon, CMMIRK-M34,132.3495

and serued God euer aftyr wyth all hys myght, CMMIRK-M34,132.3496

and had +te blysse of Heuen.  The wheche blysse God graunte you and me.
CMMIRK-M34,132.3497

Amen.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3498

<heading>

31.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3500

DE FESTO SANCTI GEORGII, MARTYRIS.  CMMIRK-M34,132.3501

<$$heading>

Good men and woymen, such a day +ge schull haue +te fest of Saynt George.
+Te wheche day +ge schull come to holy chyrch.  in <P_133> worschyp of
God and of +tat holy martyr Seynt George +tat bo+gt his day full dere.
CMMIRK-M34,133.3503

For as I rede in hys lyfe, I fynde +tat +ter was an horrybull dragon,
+tat men of +te cyte wer so aferd, +tat +tay, by cownsell of the kyng,
yche day, +geuen hym a schepe and a chyld forto ete; for he shuld not
come into +te cyte and ete hom.  CMMIRK-M34,133.3504

Then when all +te chyldyr of +ta cyte wer eten, for bycause +tat
+te kyng +gaf hom +tat consell, +tay constrayned hym +tat had but on
doghtyr forto +geue hyr to +te dragon, as +tay had hor chyldyr before.
CMMIRK-M34,133.3505

Then +te kyng, for fere of +te pepull, wyth wepyng and gret sorow makyng,
delyuerd hom hys doghtyr yn hyr best aray.  CMMIRK-M34,133.3506

Then +tay settyn hur yn +te place +ter +tay wer wont to set o+tyr chyldyr
, and a schepe wyth hyr, forto abyde +te tyme tyll +te dragon wold come.
CMMIRK-M34,133.3507

But +ten, by ordenance of God, Seynt George come rydyng +tat way;
CMMIRK-M34,133.3508

and when he saw +te aray of +tys damesell, hym +toght well +tat hyt
schuld be a womon of gret renon, CMMIRK-M34,133.3509

and askyd hur why scho stode +ter wyth soo mornyng a chere.
CMMIRK-M34,133.3510

+Ten vnswared scho CMMIRK-M34,133.3511

and sayde:'Gentyll kny+gt, well may I be of heuy chere, +tat am a
kyngys doghtyr of +tys cyte, and am sette here forto be deuoured anon
of an horrybull dragon +tat ha+te eton all +te chyldyr of +tys cyte.
CMMIRK-M34,133.3512

And for all ben eten, now most I be eten; CMMIRK-M34,133.3513

for my fadyr +gaf +te cyte +tat consell.  Wherfor, gentyll knyght
, gos hens fast and saue +tyselfe, lest he les +te as he woll me!
'CMMIRK-M34,133.3514

'Damesell,'quod George,'+tat wer a gret vyleny to me, +tat am a
kny+gt well i-armed, yf I schuld fle, and +tou +tat art a woman schuld
abyde. 'CMMIRK-M34,133.3515

Then wyth +tys worde, +te horrybull best put vp his hed, spyttyng out
fure, CMMIRK-M34,133.3516

and proferet batayll to George.  CMMIRK-M34,133.3517

+Ten made George a cros befor hym, CMMIRK-M34,133.3518

and set hys spere in +te grate, CMMIRK-M34,133.3519

and wyth such myght bare down +te dragon into +te erth, +tat he bade
+tis damysell bynd hur gurdull about his necke and lede hym aftyr hur
into +te cyte.  CMMIRK-M34,133.3520

Then +tys dragon sewet her forth, as hyt had ben a gentyll hownde,
mekly wythout any mysdoyng.  CMMIRK-M34,133.3521

But when +te pepull of +te cyte saw +te dragon come, +tay floen, ych
man into hys hyrn, for ferd.  CMMIRK-M34,133.3522

Then callyd George +te pepull a+geyne, CMMIRK-M34,133.3523

and bade +tay schuld not be aferd; CMMIRK-M34,133.3524

for yf +tay wolden leue in Crist and take fologht, he wold befor hom
all sle hym, <P_134> and so delyuer hom of hor enmy.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3525

Then wer +tay all so glad, +tat xx=ti= +towsand of men, wythout woymen
and chyldren, wer folowed, CMMIRK-M34,134.3526

and +te kyng was fyrst folowed and all hys houshold.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3527

+Ten George slogh +tys dragon, CMMIRK-M34,134.3528

and bade bryng x exen to hym, and draw hym out of +te cyte, +tat +te
sauer of hym schuld do hom no greue.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3529

And bade +te kyng byld fast in euery hurne of hys lond chyrches, and be
lusty forto here Godys seruyce, and do honour to all men of holy chrych
, and euer haue mynd and compassion of all men +tat wer nedy and pore.
CMMIRK-M34,134.3530

Then, when +tat George had +tus turnyd +tys lond to Godis fay+te,
he herd how +te Emperour Dyaclisian dyd mony cristen men to de+t.
CMMIRK-M34,134.3531

Then he went to hym boldely, CMMIRK-M34,134.3532

and repreued hym of +te cursed dede.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3533

Then +te Emperour anon commawndyd forto do hym into prison and lay hym
+ter vpryght, and a mylne-ston vpon his brest, forto haue so cruschet
hym to de+t.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3534

But when he was seruet so, he prayd to God of help; CMMIRK-M34,134.3535

and God kept hym so, +tat he feld no harme yn no party of hys body.
CMMIRK-M34,134.3536

But when +te Emperour herd +terof, he bade make a whele set full of
howkes yn +tat on syde of +te whele, and swerde poyntys in +tat o+tyr
syde a+geyne +tat, and set George in +te myddys, and so forto turne +te
wheles and all torase hys body on ay+tyr syde.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3537

But when he was yn +te turment, he prayd to Crist of socour,
CMMIRK-M34,134.3538

and was holpen anon.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3539

Aftyr he was put in an hote brennyng lyme-kylne and closed +teryn,
forto haue ben brent; CMMIRK-M34,134.3540

but God turnet wyth hys my+gt +te hete into cold dew.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3541

+Gette, +te +tryd day aftyr, when all men wendon he had ben brent to
coles, +ten was he fonde lyght and mery, CMMIRK-M34,134.3542

and +tonked God.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3543

Aftyr when he was fatte and sette before +te Emperour, he repreuyd hym
of hys false goddys, CMMIRK-M34,134.3544

and sayde +tay wer but fendys, and wythout myght, and false at nede.
CMMIRK-M34,134.3545

Then made +tys Emperour forto bete his mou+te wyth stonys, tyll hyt was
all topounet, CMMIRK-M34,134.3546

and made to bete hys body wyth dry bolle-senows, tyll +te flessch fell
from +te bon and hys guttes myght be seyne.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3547

+Get aftyr +tay made hym to drynke venom +tat was made strong for +te
nonys, forto haue poysont hym to +te de+t anon.  CMMIRK-M34,134.3548

But when George had made +te syngne of +te cros on hit, he dranke hyt
wythout any greve, soo +tat, for wondyr +terof, +te man +tat <P_135>
made +te poysen, anon turned to the fay+te, and anon was don to de+te
for Crystys sake.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3549

Then, +te ny+gt aftyr, as George was in prison prayng to God, God come
to hym wyth gret lyght, CMMIRK-M34,135.3550

and bade hym be of good comfort; CMMIRK-M34,135.3551

for in +te morow he schuld make an end of hys passyon, CMMIRK-M34,135.3552

and so com to hym into +te ioy +tat euer schall last.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3553

And when he had set a crown of gold apon hys hed, he +gaf hym hys
blessyng CMMIRK-M34,135.3554

and stegh into Heuen.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3555

Then anon, on +te morow, for he wold not do sacryfice to +te Emperourys
false goddys, he made to smyte of hys hed; CMMIRK-M34,135.3556

and soo passed to God.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3557

And when +te Emperour wold haue gone to hys palys, +te layte fure brent
hym and all hys seruantes.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3558

<heading>

Narracio.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3560

<$$heading>

In a story of Antioch ys wrytton +tat, when cristen men beseget Ierusalem
, a fayre +gong kny+gt aperut to a prest, CMMIRK-M34,135.3562

and sayde +tat he was Saynt George and leder of cristen men,
CMMIRK-M34,135.3563

and commaundyd +tat he schuld bere wyth hom hys relykes, and com wyth
hom to +te sege.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3564

But when +tay comen to +te walles of Ierusalem, +te Saracens weren
so strong wythyn +tat cristen men durst not clymbe vp hor laddres.
CMMIRK-M34,135.3565

Then com Seynt George, clo+tyd yn whyte, and a red crosse on hys brest ,
CMMIRK-M34,135.3566

and +gode vp +te laddyrs, CMMIRK-M34,135.3567

and bade +te cristen men com aftyr hym.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3568

And so wyth +te helpe of Seynt George, +tay wonen +te cyte,
CMMIRK-M34,135.3569

and slogh all +te Saresyns +tay fonden +teryn.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3570

And +terfor pray we to Saynt George +tat he wyll be our helpe at oure
nede, and saue +tys reem to +te worschyp of God and his modyr Mary and
all +te company of Heuen.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3571

Amen.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3572

<heading>

32.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3574

DE SANCI MARCO SERMO BREUIS.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3575

<$$heading>

Good men and woymen, such a day +ge schall haue Seynt Marcus day, +tat was
on of +te foure +tat wryton +te gospellys, and prechet hom to +te pepull.
CMMIRK-M34,135.3577

Then was +tys Marke furst an he+ten man, CMMIRK-M34,135.3578

but aftyr he was folowet of Seynt Petyr CMMIRK-M34,135.3579

and soo sewet Petyr long aftyr, tyll he was full ta+gt in +te byleue.
CMMIRK-M34,135.3580

And when he was full ylurned of Cristys fay+te, +ten Seynt Petyr made
hym goo and prech +te pepull Godys word.  CMMIRK-M34,135.3581

And for he was soo holy a man, +te pepull allgate wold make hym a prest,
he, for gret <P_136> mekenes of hymselfe, made to kyt of his +tombe;
CMMIRK-M34,136.3582

neuer+teles when God wold haue hyt, Seynt Petyr wyth gret instaunce made
hym to take +te ordyr of prest.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3583

Then was he besy day and ny+gt forto prech Godys word to +te pepull;
CMMIRK-M34,136.3584

and all +tat he sayde wyth worde, he confermed wyth good ensampull and
wyth doyng of myracles.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3585

Thus, by inspyracyon of +te Holy Gost, he +gode to +te cyte of
Alysandyr, forto turne +te pepull of +te cyte to +te fay+t of Crist.
CMMIRK-M34,136.3586

Then when he come into +te cyte, at +te forme fote +tat he set yn at
+te +gate, hys scho+g barst CMMIRK-M34,136.3587

and was toren; wherby he wyst well +tat he schuld not go from +tens,
but +tat he schuld take hys ende +ter: CMMIRK-M34,136.3588

and soo dyd.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3589

Then, when he com ynto +te cyte, he saw a man clowtyng pore men schone
+tat werne torne; CMMIRK-M34,136.3590

and +to+g +tis man wer a panyme, he was cristen yn hys doyng.
Wherfor Saynt Marke prayde forto amende his schone +tat wer torne.
CMMIRK-M34,136.3591

+Ten +tis man, for he saw +tat Marke was pore, and nedy, and of sympull
aray, hym +to+gt +tat hyt was almys forto helpe hym, CMMIRK-M34,136.3592

and toke hys schone to hym, CMMIRK-M34,136.3593

and began forto sawe on hit.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3594

And as he sewet full helt, by Godis ordenance, he wondyd hym-selfe in
+te honde wyth his nalle grevesly; CMMIRK-M34,136.3595

and so, what for ache and penance +tat he had +terof, among his woo he
called helpe of God.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3596

And when Saynt Marke herd +tat, he +tonkyd God; CMMIRK-M34,136.3597

and anon he spytte in +te er+te, CMMIRK-M34,136.3598

and makyd fene, CMMIRK-M34,136.3599

and wyth +tat fen anoynted +te mannys hond in +te name of Ihesu Crist:
CMMIRK-M34,136.3600

and anon he was hole.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3601

Then, when +tys man segh such vertu yn Saynt Marke, he prayde hym forto
dwell wyth hym.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3602

Then Marke dwelled wyth +tys man CMMIRK-M34,136.3603

and preched hym, so +tat he folewet hym and all hys howshold;
CMMIRK-M34,136.3604

and aftur for gret holynes.  +tat he saw yn hym, he made +tys man
a byschop.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3605

Thus when men of +te cyte seen how Marke preched +te fayth of Crist,
and dyspysyd hor fals goddys, they token hym, CMMIRK-M34,136.3606

and tyed hym by +te neke wyth a rope, CMMIRK-M34,136.3607

and drewen hym on +te stonys, cryyng yfere in despyte of hym:'Draw we
+tys bugull to +te bygulstede! 'CMMIRK-M34,136.3608

So when tay had drawen hym negh to +te de+te, +ten +tay putten hym ynto
+te prison tyll on +te morow.  CMMIRK-M34,136.3609

+Ten <P_137> com +tat ny+gt Crist into +te prison to hym
CMMIRK-M34,137.3610

and sayde:'Pes be to +te, Marke our euangelyst, CMMIRK-M34,137.3611

be no+gt agast; CMMIRK-M34,137.3612

for I am wyth +te! 'CMMIRK-M34,137.3613

Then on +te morow +tey come a+geyn, CMMIRK-M34,137.3614

and fat hym out a+geyn, CMMIRK-M34,137.3615

and drewen hym tyll he was ded.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3616

And when he felde +tat he schuld dye, he sayd:'In manus tuas, Domine,
commendo spiritum meum, redimisti'; CMMIRK-M34,137.3617

and so +terwyth +gaf vp hys gost.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3618

Then aftyr, when +tay wold haue brent hys body for malyce, anon +ter
come such a powdyr and layte and er+te-qwake, +tat no man durst abyde,
CMMIRK-M34,137.3619

but all fleen away.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3620

+Ten yn +te ny+gt aftyr Cristen men token hys body, CMMIRK-M34,137.3621

and buryet hyt wyth gret worschyp, as hyt was worthy.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3622

Then fell hyt soo aftyr +tat yche contrey halowet Seynt Markeys day, saue
on contrey the whech was callyd Appuleo.  +Te whech contrey was so desesut
by hete and vnkynd dro+gt, +tat all +te cornes and frutys faylut hom,
+tat +tay wer negh enfamyscht for defaute of corne.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3623

But +ten come +ter a voyce from Heuen, CMMIRK-M34,137.3624

and bade halow Saynt Markeys day, as o+tyr crysten men duden,
CMMIRK-M34,137.3625

and +ten schuld +tay be releuet.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3626

And when +tay dydden soo, God send to hom all maner of frutys.
CMMIRK-M34,137.3627

Now, good men and woymen, +ge haue herd of +tis seyntis lyfe, and why
hys day ys halowet; CMMIRK-M34,137.3628

+ten hit is nedfull to tell you why +ge schull fast his day and goo
in processyon.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3629

<heading>

Narracio.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3631

<$$heading>

I rede +tat in +te cyte of Rome on +tis day fell such a qwalme and soden
deth among +te pepull of +te cyte, +tat when a man gonet o+tyr neset,
anon +terwyth he +gaf vp +te gost; CMMIRK-M34,137.3633

and o+tyr deydyn sodenly a gret nownbyr.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3634

Then +te pope Pelagius bade ych man, when he gonet, to make a cros on
his mou+te; CMMIRK-M34,137.3635

and when a man herd ano+tyr nese, he schuld bydde:'Crist helpe +te!
'CMMIRK-M34,137.3636

and so mony wern sauet.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3637

And also he made +te pepull fast, and to go about in procession barfot,
and soo pray holy seyntys of Heuen forto pray for hom to God, +tat he
of his goodnes schuld haue mercy of hom; CMMIRK-M34,137.3638

and soo dyd.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3639

Then come aftyr Seynt Gregory, CMMIRK-M34,137.3640

and made hom do +te same ych +gere on Saynt Markeys day, bo+te fast and
go on processyon, CMMIRK-M34,137.3641

and canonysyt hit, forto be don alway aftyr.  CMMIRK-M34,137.3642

Then come aftyr a pope was <P_138> called Liberius, CMMIRK-M34,138.3643

and segh how +te frute of +te erth and of tren, for $tendyrnes of
homselfe, token at +tys day ofte-tyme gret harme, what by +tondyr and by
layte, by vnkynde hete, be vnkynd stormys, by whyrlyng-wynde, by mystes,
by myldewys, be grene wormys, be long-taylet fleys.  CMMIRK-M34,138.3644

And also, for +te pepull to sone aftyr +te receyuyng of hor howsyll
turnet a+geyne to synne, hauyng no reward to +tat hegh sacrament,
+terfor God send vengeans among +te pepull mor +tat tyme of +te +gere
+ten ano+tyr, of pestylens, of werres, of der+tes, of dyuerse sekenes.
Wherfor +tys holy pope, forto put away Godys wra+t from +te pepull,
he commaundet all cristen men and woymen forto halow +tys day, and fast
not to certeyne +geres as lewde pepull tellyth, but allway forth on, and
forto come +tat day to +te chyrch, and goo on pro-cession wyth +te letany.
Wherfor, good men, +ge schull wete well +tat all +tylke +tat don a+geyne
+te constytucyons of holy chyrche wytyng, he ys acurset tyll he come to
amendement; CMMIRK-M34,138.3645

and yf he dey yn +tat curs vnschryuen, he is dampnet fore euer befor God.
CMMIRK-M34,138.3646

Herefor, good men and woymen, I charch you on holy chyrche byhalfe,
+tat +ge fast +tat day, but hit fall on a Sonenday o+tyr yn Astyr weke ;
CMMIRK-M34,138.3647

and comyth +tat day to +te chyrch; CMMIRK-M34,138.3648

and heruth God seruyce as cristen men owen forto do; CMMIRK-M34,138.3649

and pray+te hertly to Seynt Marke +tat he woll pray for you to God forto
put away all myscheues of body and of soule, and +tat +ge may haue +te
blys +tat he bo+gt you to.  To +to whech blys God bryng you and me to,
yf hyt be hys will.  CMMIRK-M34,138.3650

Amen.  CMMIRK-M34,138.3651

33.  CMMIRK-M34,138.3653

DE FESTO APOSTOLORUM PHILIPPI ET IACOBI ET EORUM SOLEMPNITATE.
CMMIRK-M34,138.3654

<$$heading>

Good men and woymen, such a day {TEXT:N} +ge schull haue an hegh fest in
holy $chyrch: Seynt Phelypys day and Seynt Iacobs, Cristys holy apostolys.
CMMIRK-M34,138.3656

But for +tys comy+t wythyn +te tyme of Astyr seruyce, +ge schull not
fast +te euen; CMMIRK-M34,138.3657

but comyth to +te chyrch as Godys owne pepull, to worschyp God and his
holy apostolys.  CMMIRK-M34,138.3658

Then schull +ge know +tat +tys Phylyp was send by all +tat o+tyr apostolys
into a contre +tat was called Cythya, forto prech Godis <P_139> worde
to +te vnbeleued pepull.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3659

But when he come +tedyr, and preched a+geyn hor mawmetys, preuyng +tat
+tay wer fendys, and not goddys, anon +tys mysbeleued pepull token +tys
holy apostull, CMMIRK-M34,139.3660

and ladden hym ynto hor tempull, CMMIRK-M34,139.3661

and constrayned hym to do sacryfyce to hor mawmetys, CMMIRK-M34,139.3662

o+tir ellys he schuld be ded.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3663

Then, as +tay wern besy forto haue done +tys doses, sodenly a gret dragon
com out of +te er+te, CMMIRK-M34,139.3664

and slogh +tre of +tes mysbeleued men, CMMIRK-M34,139.3665

and venemet so +te pepull wyth hys bre+tyng, +tat +ter fell on hom all
such a sekenes, +tat for woo and passyon +tat +tay hadon, +tay cryed
all waylyng and wepyng yche on to $o+tyr.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3666

Then sayde Phelyp to hom:'+Gyf +ge woll be helyd of your sekenes +tat
greue+te you, and also +tes men be bro+gt a+geyne to lyve +tat ben
ded, castys don +tes mawmetys +tat +ge wolden haue me to worschyp,
CMMIRK-M34,139.3667

and setty+te +ter a cros lyke to +te cros +tat my maystyr dyed apon,
CMMIRK-M34,139.3668

and worschyp hyt. 'CMMIRK-M34,139.3669

Then dyd +tay so gladly and fayn, forto be holpen of hor woo +tat greuet
hom soo sore.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3670

And when +tay hadden soo don, anon ry+gt +tay wern all hole;
CMMIRK-M34,139.3671

and Saynt Phelyp, be callyng of Cristys nome, reryd vp a+geyne to lyue
+tre men +tat wern ded.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3672

And when he had don soo, he commaundyd +te dragon forto go into
wyldernes $+ter $as {TEXT:+teras} he schuld neuer greue man ny best;
CMMIRK-M34,139.3673

and so +gode forth, CMMIRK-M34,139.3674

and was neuer seen aftyr.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3675

Thus when Seynt Phelyp had preched +te pepull, and made hom stedfast
in +te fay+te of Ihesu Crist, and +gode forth into a cyte Ieropolym;
CMMIRK-M34,139.3676

and for he prechet +te fay+te of Ihesu Crist +tat was don on +te cros,
+terfor wykked men of +tat cyte token hym, CMMIRK-M34,139.3677

and dydden hym on a cros, as Crist was, CMMIRK-M34,139.3678

and soo payned hym to +te de+te.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3679

And soo he +gode to Crist, hys maystyr, forto dwell wy+te hym in +te
ioy +tat neuer schall haue ende.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3680

Now +ge schull here of Seynt Iacob, +tat was called among +te apostolys
'Iamys +te lasse,'forto be know from'Iamys +te more'+tat was Seynt
Ionys bro+tyr.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3681

But +tys Iacob, o+tyr Iames, +tat ys all on name, was called Cristys
bro+tyr; CMMIRK-M34,139.3682

for he was soo lyke to Crist, +tat when +te Iewes token oure Lord Crist
, +tay cow+te not know +tat on by +tat o+tyr, but as Iudas trayde Crist
by a cosse, and soo ta+gt hom to hym.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3683

Thys Iamys was soo holy from +te tyme +tat he was borne, all +te tyme
of hys lyfe, +tat he dranke no wyne ny syser ne ale; CMMIRK-M34,139.3684

for +tys $+tere nys non yn +tat contrey.  CMMIRK-M34,139.3685
